=A1=B0python setup.py install=A1=B1

=20

You need python 2.4, cherrypy 3.x and python-pam-0.4.2. All available =
with
Ubuntu=A1=AFs package manager.

CentOS/Redhat users will have to Google. Sorry.

=20

The archive is just an svn checkout of =A1=B0trunk=A1=B1, with my =
changes applied,
so as of now it is based on the latest code.

=20

Good luck.

<div class=3DSection1>

<p class=3DMsoNormal>Greetings.<o:p></o:p></p>

<p class=3DMsoNormal><o:p> </o:p></p>

<p class=3DMsoNormal>More updates from me. <o:p></o:p></p>

<p class=3DMsoNormal>I still can=A1=AFt check in to subversion (I have =
tried),
so instructions on how to try my fixes will follow later.<o:p></o:p></p>

<p class=3DMsoNormal><o:p> </o:p></p>

<p class=3DMsoNormal>All the work I have done is based on the TODO list =
on the
roadmap<o:p></o:p></p>

<p class=3DMsoNormal><a
href=3D"http://www.rdiffweb.org/wiki/index.php?title=3DRoadmap">http://ww=
w.rdiffweb.org/wiki/index.php?title=3DRoadmap</a><o:p></o:p></p>

<p class=3DMsoNormal><o:p> </o:p></p>

<p class=3DMsoNormal>First; What I have changed:<o:p></o:p></p>

<p class=3DMsoNormal>The init script  (as in =A1=B0service =
rdiff-web start=A1=B1)<o:p></o:p></p>

<p class=3DMsoNormal>Now honours stop, start and status. <o:p></o:p></p>

<p class=3DMsoNormal>Stop and start check whether they have succeeded =
and report
an appropriate message and exit code<o:p></o:p></p>

<p class=3DMsoNormal><o:p> </o:p></p>

<p class=3DMsoNormal>rdiff-web-config is now a little more =
sane.<o:p></o:p></p>

<p class=3DMsoNormal>If an old rdw.conf file exists, its values are =
taken as the
default.<o:p></o:p></p>

<p class=3DMsoNormal>You also have a nice list of what you can do with =
users
existing.<o:p></o:p></p>

<p class=3DMsoNormal><o:p> </o:p></p>

<p class=3DMsoNormal>Authentication<o:p></o:p></p>

<p class=3DMsoNormal>You now have the option of using PAM (the Unix =
users/passwords).
This is currently not working on Centos5.2, but works fine on =
Ubuntu.<o:p></o:p></p>

<p class=3DMsoNormal>(You can still use the internal RDW users on any =
system).<o:p></o:p></p>

<p class=3DMsoNormal>When PAM is enabled the administrators can=A1=AFt =
change
other user=A1=AFs password (this would violate unix security), but every =
user
can change their own password.<o:p></o:p></p>

<p class=3DMsoNormal><o:p> </o:p></p>

<p class=3DMsoNormal>Directory listing<o:p></o:p></p>

<p class=3DMsoNormal>You can now sort the display by Name, size, date or =
number
of old versions.<o:p></o:p></p>

<p class=3DMsoNormal>Just click on the appropriate heading to sort, =
click again
to reverse the sort.<o:p></o:p></p>

<p class=3DMsoNormal><o:p> </o:p></p>

<p class=3DMsoNormal>Previous versions<o:p></o:p></p>

<p class=3DMsoNormal>The number of previous versions is now a link to a =
page that
brings up only the old versions of that file.<o:p></o:p></p>

<p class=3DMsoNormal>Basically, if the popup/flyout is not working on =
your
browser, or is too long to be useful, just click on =A1=B0947 Previous =
Revisions=A1=B1
<o:p></o:p></p>

<p class=3DMsoNormal>for a page where you can see revision 1 and =
948.<o:p></o:p></p>

<p class=3DMsoNormal><o:p> </o:p></p>

<p class=3DMsoNormal>Annoying change:<o:p></o:p></p>

<p class=3DMsoNormal>I have had to disable SSL; I don=A1=AFt quite know =
why,
perhaps I have the wrong version of cherrypy.<o:p></o:p></p>

<p class=3DMsoNormal><o:p> </o:p></p>

<p class=3DMsoNormal>Technical change:<o:p></o:p></p>

<p class=3DMsoNormal>I have altered the template engine to honour =
=A1=B0\&=A1=B1.<o:p></o:p></p>

<p class=3DMsoNormal>Basically, if a page tries to render =A1=B0this =
& that=A1=B1,
the rdw template engine changes it to =A1=B0this &amp; =
that=A1=B1.<o:p></o:p></p>

<p class=3DMsoNormal>Now, if you try to render =A1=B0this & that =
\&hearts;=A1=B1
the template engine will produce =A1=B0this &amp; that <span
style=3D'font-family:"Arial","sans-serif"'>&hearts;=A1=B1</span> =
<o:p></o:p></p>

<p class=3DMsoNormal>(hopefully the browser will then correctly show =
=A1=B0this &
that <span =
style=3D'font-family:"Arial","sans-serif"'>=A2=BE=A1=B1)</span><o:p></o:p=
></p>

<p class=3DMsoNormal><o:p> </o:p></p>

<p class=3DMsoNormal><o:p> </o:p></p>

<p class=3DMsoNormal><o:p> </o:p></p>

<p class=3DMsoNormal>Secondly; To install:<o:p></o:p></p>

<p class=3DMsoNormal><o:p> </o:p></p>

<p class=3DMsoNormal>Extract the attached archive.<o:p></o:p></p>

<p class=3DMsoNormal>From the =A1=B0trunk=A1=B1 directory, =
do<o:p></o:p></p>

<p class=3DMsoNormal>=A1=B0python setup.py install=A1=B1<o:p></o:p></p>

<p class=3DMsoNormal><o:p> </o:p></p>

<p class=3DMsoNormal>You need python 2.4, cherrypy 3.x and =
python-pam-0.4.2. All
available with Ubuntu=A1=AFs package manager.<o:p></o:p></p>

<p class=3DMsoNormal>CentOS/Redhat users will have to Google. =
Sorry.<o:p></o:p></p>

<p class=3DMsoNormal><o:p> </o:p></p>

<p class=3DMsoNormal>The archive is just an svn checkout of =
=A1=B0trunk=A1=B1,
with my changes applied, so as of now it is based on the latest =
code.<o:p></o:p></p>

<p class=3DMsoNormal><o:p> </o:p></p>

<p class=3DMsoNormal>Good luck.<o:p></o:p></p>

</div>

</body>

</html>
